# List of supported chips

*For an explanation of the requirements tab, please have a look at [REQUIREMENTS](./REQUIREMENTS.md) document.*

## CONTENT

+ [TIVA](#tiva)
+ [NXP](#nxp)
+ [PIC32](#pic32)
+ [PIC18](#pic18)
+ [STM32](#stm32)

---
